                 </a>

               <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
                While some errors on your tax returns are honest mistakes that can be corrected, your efforts to game the system or get more of a return may teeter on the edge of outright tax fraud. Check out this information from the IRS’s website and their 2019 “Dirty Dozen” list of the worst tax scams to find out some of the ways you may be accidentally committing tax fraud.

            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['homepage_1613'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x600/300x250_3_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_300x600/300x250_3_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_3_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'homepage_1613',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_300x600/300x250_3_/',
              adType: 'cube',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.pilotonline/homepage',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[300, 600], [300, 250]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
            </script>
           </div>
          </div>
